CCT - Change Coordination Tool - Email Notification

Login to CCT to get more information about the work. Always check the Approve queue for work needing your authorization. Use the Search feature to find things. Look at the Help and Index if you don't know how to do something.

You are responsible to keep your group's contact information updated and correct in CSC, NET and CCT. Use the "Server Contacts" option under the Reports menu to help you identify where you need to go to update your contact information.

Notifications go out to all members of your NET group or CCT subscriber list team. This means that someone from your group may have already approved the work. Your Approve queue may be empty!

If you see green text next to the server below in parentheses, this information will contain your groups current status response, the persons name, and the date of they responded.

Some of these work requests are for FYI notification only, which means you are not required to approve the work, but your group wants to be informed of any pending work. (Please note the "Response Required" field in the ticket below.)

As status information changes for work, you will get updates. This doesn't mean you have to do anything. New status messages in the past 30 hours under the server names below are colored in blue and are meant to keep you informed of changes. Email notifications will only show messages from the last 48 hours. To see all the messages, login to CCT and bring up the record. Use the search tool.

CCT URL: https://cct.corp.intranet

If you discover an error or problem, please send screenshots and detail information about it to Greg Parkin (gregparkin58@gmail.com). In most cases he needs to try and recreate the error in order to fix the problem. You can also create a Remedy ticket to AIM-TOOLS-BOM and assign it to Greg.

CCT 7 is a new major release and is best viewed using Firefox or Chrome. There are always new feature requests and enhancements to make it better. Please be patient, your input is always welcome.
